Please REFUSE any vaccines that they want to give your baby at the hospital. The Hepatitis B shot is the one they've been giving newborns for a while. it isn't really necessary, and it can cause harm to your baby. Ask for a copy of the information sheet that comes with the shot and read it. Ask about it soon because they like to give it between 12 and 24 hours after birth.
